General Status
‚ö†Ô∏è DISCLAIMER (Read Me)

This report reflects only what survived the round trip back to this script, and not necessarily the **Absolute Truth of the Universe‚Ñ¢**.

Remember that between your terminal and the DNS server lies a hostile jungle inhabited by:

  • Paranoid Firewalls: Blocking even positive thoughts (and legitimate UDP packets).
  • Creative Middleboxes: Security filters that think your DNS query is a nuclear attack.
  • Rate Limits: Because nobody likes spam, not even the server.
  • Load Balancing: Where different servers answer with different moods.

Conclusion: If everything is red, breathe before cursing the DNS admin (check your network). If everything is green, be suspicious.

Help & About

üìå Disclaimer

Este relat√≥rio foi gerado automaticamente pelo FriendlyDNSReporter v1.0.17. Todas as informa√ß√µes aqui apresentadas refletem o estado da infraestrutura no momento exato da execu√ß√£o. Lat√™ncias e conectividade podem variar. A flag VER: HIDDEN indica que o servidor oculta sua vers√£o (boa pr√°tica). AXFR: DENIED indica que a transfer√™ncia de zona est√° bloqueada (seguro).

Icon Legend
‚úÖSuccess / OK / Consistent
üö´Failure / NXDOMAIN / Critical Error
‚ö†Ô∏èWarning / Divergence (Alert)

Technical Glossary
  • SOA Serial: Zone serial number (should be equal on all servers).
  • AXFR: Complete zone transfer (risk if open to all).
  • Recursion: If "Open", server resolves external names (DDoS risk).
  • DNSSEC: Cryptographic security validation for domains.
Commands and Usage (Help Text)
    clear
    echo -e "${CYAN}==============================================================================${NC}"
    echo -e "${CYAN}   üìö FriendlyDNSReporter - REFERENCE MANUAL (v${SCRIPT_VERSION})        ${NC}"
    echo -e "${CYAN}==============================================================================${NC}"
    echo -e ""
    print_help_text
    echo -e "${BLUE}==============================================================================${NC}"
